[1:13:17] Xylax: It has to do with the body's production of pheomelanin which produces blonde hair and lessens as the child ages at which time more eumelanin (melanin) is produced, causing darker, brown coloring in eyes and hair. When pigment stops being produced, as we age, hair loses all color and becomes white or grey.
